			ELSE
				RETURN
			END;
			IF y < 256 THEN
				t[tW] := SHORT(CHR(y)); INC(tW)
			ELSE
				t[tW] := SHORT(CHR(y DIV 100H)); t[tW+1] := SHORT(CHR(y MOD 100H)); INC(tW, 2)
			END;
			INC(fR); DEC(fLen)
		END
	END Encode;

	PROCEDURE NewEncoder* (): Codecs.Encoder;
		VAR e: Encoder;
	BEGIN
		NEW(e); RETURN e
	END NewEncoder;

	(* Decoder *)

	PROCEDURE (d: Decoder) Decode (IN f: ARRAY OF SHORTCHAR; VAR fR, fLen: INTEGER; VAR t: ARRAY OF CHAR; VAR tW: INTEGER; OUT state: BOOLEAN);
		VAR x, y: INTEGER;
	BEGIN
		WHILE fLen > 0 DO
			x := ORD(f[fR]);
			CASE d.st OF 0:
				CASE x OF
				| 00H..7FH: t[tW] := CHR(00H + x); INC(tW)
				| 81H..0FEH: d.b := 256 * x; INC(d.st)
				ELSE d.st := -1; RETURN END
			| 1:
				x := x + d.b;
				CASE x OF
				| 0B4C0H: y := 0B4C0H
				| 0F0ACH,0FAAEH: y := -7FFFH + x
				| 0B4C1H: y := 0B4C4H
				| 0B4C2H: y := 0B4C8H
				| 0D0C7H: y := 50D1H
				| 0DCABH: y := 5CB7H
				| 0B4C3H: y := 0B4D0H
				| 0B4C4H: y := 0B4D5H
				| 0C9E3H,0C9E4H: y := 15H + x
				| 0B4C5H,0B4C6H,0C9E5H: y := 17H + x
				| 0B4C7H: y := 0B4E0H
				| 0C9E6H: y := 0CA00H
				| 0B4C8H..0B4CCH: y := 1BH + x
				| 0EDDAH: y := 6DF8H
				| 0B4CDH,0B4CEH: y := 1FH + x
				| 0B4CFH: y := 0B4EFH
				| 0B4D0H,0C9E7H,0C9E8H,0C9EBH: y := 21H + x
				| 0C9E9H: y := 0CA0BH
				| 0C9EAH: y := 0CA0DH
				| 0CFADH: y := 4FD3H
				| 0F5ACH: y := 75D5H
				| 0E7E7H: y := 6813H
				| 0DDD9H: y := 5E06H
				| 0F1D8H: y := 7206H
				| 0E3E9H,0F4ADH: y := -7FCDH + x
				| 0EDC7H: y := 6DFBH
				| 0CAA1H,0CAA2H: y := 37H + x
				| 0CAA3H: y := 0CADCH
				| 0CAA4H: y := 0CAE0H
				| 0E3CCH,0F3A5H: y := -7FBFH + x
				| 0B4D1H,0B4D2H: y := 43H + x
				| 0C9ECH: y := 0CA30H
				| 0B4D3H: y := 0B518H
				| 0C9A1H,0CAA6H: y := 46H + x
				| 0B4D4H,0B4D5H,0C9EDH: y := 47H + x
				| 0CAA5H: y := 0CAEDH
				| 0C9A2H,0C9A3H,0C9A6H,0CAAAH: y := 4AH + x
				| 0C9A4H: y := 0C9EFH

				| 0E8B7H: y := 6904H

				| 0B4D8H: y := 0B527H

				| 0B4DBH: y := 0B52EH
				| 0F2A8H: y := 72FDH

	END Reset;
